          Olé Olé Olé! A Trip Across Latin America - Released May 26 2017<br /><br />Advanced iTunes Download: <a href="http://smarturl.it/STONESOLEDIGITAL" target="_blank" title="http://smarturl.it/STONESOLEDIGITAL" rel="nofollow" dir="ltr" class="yt-uix-redirect-link">http://smarturl.it/STONESOL...</a><br /><br />¡Olé, Olé, Olé! A Trip Across Latin America by the Rolling Stones, a documentary film by Paul Dugdale, will be released by Eagle Rock Entertainment on DVD, Blu-ray and digital download, on May 26th 2017.<br /><br />T¡Olé, Olé, Olé! A Trip Across Latin America follows the Rolling Stones on their 2016 tour through ten Latin America cities, whilst at the same time trying to stage their first ever concert in Havana, Cuba, a colossal once-in-a-lifetime open air free show, the likes of which Cuba had never seen before. The film captures the unique chemistry that exists between the Rolling Stones and their Latin American fans, a bond that has stretched across many years.<br /><br />As well as the full film, the Bonus Features on this release offer a collection of incredible full length performances from the Latin American tour:<br /><br />1) Out Of Control (Buenos Aires, Argentina)<br /><br />2) Paint It Black (Buenos Aires, Argentina)<br /><br />3) Honky Tonk Women (Sao Paulo, Brazil)<br /><br />4) Sympathy For The Devil (Sao Paulo, Brazil)<br /><br />5) You Got The Silver (Lima, Peru)<br /><br />6) Midnight Rambler (Lima, Peru)<br /><br />7) Miss You (Lima, Peru)<br /><br />Featuring electrifying live performances, intimate moments with the band members, anticipation and reaction from the fans, and all the twists and turns of staging the Havana concert !Olé, Olé, Olé! A Trip Across Latin America is a portrait of a vital band still at the very top of their game.<br /><br />Subscribe for more: <a                     <div class="shelf-wrapper clearfix">
          <div class="compact-shelf shelf-item yt-uix-shelfslider yt-uix-shelfslider-at-head yt-uix-shelfslider-at-tail vve-check clearfix c4-visible-on-hover-container  yt-section-hover-container yt-uix-tdl"  data-sessionlink="ei=tW_3WL65Kcjn8gT4m7CACg&amp;ved=CLsBENwcGAIiEwj-57ei2bDTAhXIs5wKHfgNDKAomxw">
            <h2 class="branded-page-module-title">
      <a href="/playlist?list=PLIEx7PjdcpR7WwdhMZAtYFGRO9MrNpNFy" class="yt-uix-sessionlink branded-page-module-title-link spf-nolink" data-sessionlink="ei=tW_3WL65Kcjn8gT4m7CACg&amp;ved=CM4BEM4eIhMI_ue3otmw0wIVyLOcCh34DQygKJsc">
            <span class="branded-page-module-title-text">
      <span class="" >Blue And Lonesome - Out Now!</span>
    </span>

      </a>
        <a href="/watch?v=qEuV82GqQnE&amp;list=PLIEx7PjdcpR7WwdhMZAtYFGRO9MrNpNFy" class="yt-uix-button  shelves-play play-all-icon-btn yt-uix-sessionlink yt-uix-button-default yt-uix-button-size-small yt-uix-button-has-icon no-icon-markup" data-sessionlink="ei=tW_3WL65Kcjn8gT4m7CACg"><span class="yt-uix-button-content">Play all</span></a>

  </h2>


        <div class="shelf-description yt-ui-ellipsis yt-ui-ellipsis-2">
        <a href="http://www.rollingstones.com/blueandlonesome/" target="_blank" title="http://www.rollingstones.com/blueandlonesome/" rel="nofollow" dir="ltr" class="yt-uix-redirect-link">http://www.rollingstones.com/blueandlonesome/</a><br /><br />On 2nd December 2016, The Rolling Stones released ‘Blue &amp; Lonesome’, their first studio album in over a decade. ‘Blue &amp; Lonesome’ takes the band back to their roots and the passion for blues music which has always been at the heart and soul of The Rolling Stones.<br /><br />The album was produced by Don Was and The Glimmer Twins and was recorded over the course of just three days in December last year at British Grove Studios in West London, just a stone’s throw from Richmond and Eel Pie Island where the Stones started out as a young blues band playing pubs and clubs. Their approach to the album was that it should be spontaneous and played live in the studio without overdubs. The band – Mick Jagger (vocals &amp; harp), Keith Richards (guitar), Charlie Watts (drums), and Ronnie Wood (guitar) were joined by their long time touring sidemen Darryl Jones (bass), Chuck Leavell (keyboards) and Matt Clifford (keyboards) and, for two of the twelve tracks, by old friend Eric Clapton, who happened to be in the next studio making his own album.<br /><br />‘Blue &amp; Lonesome’ sees the Rolling Stones tipping their hats to their early days as a blues band when they played the music of Jimmy Reed, Willie Dixon, Eddie Taylor, Little Walter and Howlin’ Wolf – artists whose songs are featured on this album.<br /><br />“This album is manifest testament to the purity of their love for making music, and the blues is, for the Stones, the fountainhead of everything they do.” Don Was, Co-Producer of ‘Blue &amp; Lonesome’
    </div>
